Dream Corridor, in fact, the promenade-style coconut grove near the hotel is more beautiful than the Coconut Dream Corridor guided by the navigation. I stayed in a sea view room. From the balcony, I can not only enjoy the hotel‚Äôs garden scenery and azure swimming pool, but also listen to The wind and sea view; the hotel rooms are quite large and have complete facilities. The faucets and other facilities are all made of copper. If you like to soak in hot springs, there is a hot spring bathtub on the balcony, so you can enjoy it to your heart's content. I stayed at the Gai Hotel for one night on January 2 and it felt good. After returning to Sanya after two days of traveling elsewhere, I chose this hotel without hesitation. If there is any shortcoming in the hotel, it is that the decoration style is a bit old-fashioned and not modern and bright enough, but in terms of value for money, this is nothing.
